vertical-align: -0.053em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.058em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi mathvariant="normal">Z</mi><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">n</mi><mo>+</mo></msup></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-5">\rm Zn^+</script></span>&nbsp;আয়ন গঠন করে</p>
</label>
                                                <span class="fas fa-check"></span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: Zn d-ব্লক মৌল হলেও অবস্থান্তর মৌল নয়। Zn ২ টি ইলেকট্রন ত্যাগ করে <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-6-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>Z</mi><msup><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>n</mi><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mn>2</mn><mo>+</mo></mrow></msup></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-33" style="width: 2.174em;                                         <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>Ni প্রভাবকের উপস্থিতিতে কত তাপমাত্রায় Xe&nbsp;ও <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-28-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><msub><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>F</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-234" style="width: 1.343em;                                         <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>নিচের কোন মৌলের d&nbsp;অরবিটাল ইলেকট্রন দ্বারা পূর্ণ থাকে?</p>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: Cd মৌলের d&nbsp;অরবিটাল ইলেকট্রন দ্বারা পূর্ণ থাকে। অর্থাৎ <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-37-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>C</mi><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>d</mi><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>(</mo><mn>48</mn><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>)</mo><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>&amp;#x2192;</mo><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>K</mi><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>r</mi><mn>4</mn><msup><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>d</mi><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mn>10</mn></mrow></msup><mn>5</mn><msup><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>s</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-297" style="width: 9.018em;                                         <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: পানিতে আর্দ্রবিশ্লেষণে-&nbsp;</p>

                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-58-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>C</mi><msup><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>r</mi><mrow class=&quot;MJX-TeXAtom-ORD&quot;><mn>6</mn><mo>+</mo></mrow></msup></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-519" style="width: 2.133em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.723em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.027em, 1001.72em, 2.133em, -999.998em); top: -1.965em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-520"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-521" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">C</span><span class="msubsup" id="MathJax-Span-522"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 1.355em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.445em, 1000.37em, 4.141em, -999.998em); top: -4.014em; left: 0em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-523" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">r</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -4.383em; left: 0.412em;"><span class="texatom" id="MathJax-Span-524"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-525"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-526" style="font-size: 70.7%; কিন্তু Cr বা যেকোনো মৌলের জারণ সংখ্যা = 0&nbsp;।<br>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Boost অর্থ ‘প্রচার করা’ এর বিপরীত হলো Restrain যার অর্থ সংযত করা। অপর পক্ষে Raise অর্থ বৃদ্ধি, Depreciate অর্থ অবমূল্যায়ন এবং Trim অর্থ ছাঁটা।</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>
